Thanks to pre-built professional templates, you don’t need any design skills to create an amazing presentation. Let’s look at three marketing presentation examples and learn how to customize each slide in seconds.</p>\n<p>Marketing plans should be visual. Anyone who’s suffered through long presentations understands the importance of diverse slide content. </p>\n<p>Elements like images, charts, and infographics help to break up the monotony of a slide deck. They’re also key to explaining complex concepts and presenting data in style.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/marketing-plan-vol-2-RWF4UN\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/988/posts/34780/image/marketing-plan-powerpoint-example.jpg\" alt=\"Marketing Plan PowerPoint Example\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"583px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/988/posts/34780/image/marketing-plan-powerpoint-example.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/988/posts/34780/image/marketing-plan-powerpoint-example.jpg\" alt=\"Marketing Plan PowerPoint Example\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"437px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/988/posts/34780/image/marketing-plan-powerpoint-example.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/988/posts/34780/image/marketing-plan-powerpoint-example.jpg\" alt=\"Marketing Plan PowerPoint Example\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"258px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/988/posts/34780/image/marketing-plan-powerpoint-example.jpg 2x\"></a></figure>\n<p>In this section, we'll use <strong><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/marketing-plan-vol-2-RWF4UN\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Marketing Plan Volume 2</a>,</strong> a multipurpose <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/presentation-templates/marketing/compatible-with-powerpoint\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">marketing presentation template</a> from Envato Elements.</p>\n<h3>1. The Intro Slide</h3>\n<p>Let’s begin by customizing a simple image-and-text slide. This one's near the beginning of the presentation, so it’s well-placed to introduce your team and roll out your marketing plan slogan.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/marketing-plan-vol-2-RWF4UN\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/1-updated.jpg\" alt=\"The Intro Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"496px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/1-updated.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/1-updated.jpg\" alt=\"The Intro Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"373px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/1-updated.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/1-updated.jpg\" alt=\"The Intro Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"222px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/1-updated.jpg 2x\"></a>\n<figcaption>Use an intro slide to set up your presentation for success.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n<p>Outlining your slogan and guiding principles early sets the stage for the balance of the presentation. It places your message into context. When your audience knows your motivations, they’re more likely to engage, understand, and follow along.</p>\n<p>The text is easily replaced. Simply click to select it, then type over it with your own words. Freely adjust the font size and styling up on PowerPoint’s ribbon. Then, add in your own photo. </p>\n<p>The placeholders in this marketing plan presentation template make this a breeze. Just click in the gray box, navigate to your image, and click to Insert it. PowerPoint will drop it onto the slide, already perfectly scaled and ready to share.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/marketing-plan-vol-2-RWF4UN\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/Tutorial%202.jpg\" alt=\"Intro Slide Finished\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"498px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/Tutorial%202.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/Tutorial%202.jpg\" alt=\"Intro Slide Finished\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"374px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/Tutorial%202.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/Tutorial%202.jpg\" alt=\"Intro Slide Finished\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"222px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/Tutorial%202.jpg 2x\"></a>\n<figcaption>Just add your text and a photo to the placeholder to create a strong intro.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n<h3>2. The Charts and Graphs Slide</h3>\n<p>Charts truly are the best way to illustrate numerical data. And thanks to PowerPoint, they can be created and edited in seconds. This slide includes a pre-built column chart with data already included. </p>\n<p>Naturally, you’ll need to customize it with your own numbers. To do that, right-click on one of the bars and then select <strong>Edit Data</strong>. PowerPoint will launch an embedded Excel spreadsheet right inside the app. There, easily type in your own data. The chart will scale and resize automatically with every change you make.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/marketing-plan-vol-2-RWF4UN\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/Tutorial%203.jpg\" alt=\"Charts and Graphs Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"661px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/Tutorial%203.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/Tutorial%203.jpg\" alt=\"Charts and Graphs Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"495px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/Tutorial%203.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/Tutorial%203.jpg\" alt=\"Charts and Graphs Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"291px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/Tutorial%203.jpg 2x\"></a>\n<figcaption>Customize charts and graphs by right clicking on the object and choosing <strong>Edit Data</strong>.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n<h3>3. Device Mockups</h3>\n<p>Finally, let’s check out device mockups. Device mockups help you showcase your website or app on representations of real devices. You’ll find mockups for smartwatches, phones, computers, tablets, and more.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/marketing-plan-vol-2-RWF4UN\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/4-updated.jpg\" alt=\"Device Mockups\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"497px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/4-updated.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/4-updated.jpg\" alt=\"Device Mockups\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"374px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/4-updated.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/4-updated.jpg\" alt=\"Device Mockups\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"222px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/4-updated.jpg 2x\"></a>\n<figcaption>Start with a device mockup template to drop your app specifics into it.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n<p>As you can see, this mockup slide focuses on a smartphone. The centerpiece is the mockup itself, the 3D representation of the device. Beside it, you can see plenty of text placeholders, in which you can provide details about the app or website. Whether your marketing PPT features digital ads, or exists to sell a digital product, mockups can be a crucial element when communicating your plan.</p>\n<p>To customize a mockup slide, you’ll first need to capture a screenshot on a real device. Transfer it to your computer and then add it to the mockup. Click on the image placeholder inside the phone screen, browse to your screenshot, and click to insert it. PowerPoint will import the image, scaling it automatically to fit inside the mockup. From there, easily swap the placeholders for your own text to create a compelling marketing PPT slide.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/marketing-plan-vol-2-RWF4UN\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/5-updated.jpg\" alt=\"Device Mockup Finished\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"497px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/5-updated.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/5-updated.jpg\" alt=\"Device Mockup Finished\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"374px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/5-updated.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/5-updated.jpg\" alt=\"Device Mockup Finished\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"222px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/151/posts/33237/image/5-updated.jpg 2x\"></a>\n<figcaption>You get a realistic-looking device image with your screen on it.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n<p>Thanks to Envato, building a marketing PowerPoint has never been easier. Your slide deck will be at the forefront of professional design—and you won’t need any editing skills to get there! By using one of these marketing plan presentation templates, you’ll have more time to work on your plan, without worrying about editing.</p>\n<p>For more on that, you’ll want to check out our helpful class=\"roundup-block__author\">Andrew Childress</div></a></li></ul>\n<h2>Inspiration: 5 Top PowerPoint (PPT) Marketing Plan Presentation Slide Designs for 2021</h2>\n<p>It's true that every marketing PowerPoint plan is going to differ. But that doesn't mean that you can't find common elements that work well for <em>every </em>marketing plan PPT. Borrowing from the best ideas is a great reason to use PPT for marketing campaign templates that already have ideas for you.</p>\n<p>Let's look at five types of slides that you'll find in many marketing PowerPoint templates. We'll sample from templates from Elements and GraphicRiver. Consider using these when you're building your marketing plan.</p>\n<h3>1. Mission Slide</h3>\n<p>A mission is that core idea that drives what you do. It's a great litmus test when you've got a new idea to measure your tactics against that mission. Does what you're doing fit with your mission? That's the question all businesses should constantly ask themselves.</p>\n<p>So, why not use a mission slide in your next marketing PowerPoint? Use a slide to capture that single idea. It creates an understanding of your goal with your audience and collaborators.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/business-plan/21284922?s_rank=7\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/our-mission-slide.jpg\" alt=\"The Mission Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"498px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/our-mission-slide.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/our-mission-slide.jpg\" alt=\"The Mission Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"374px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/our-mission-slide.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/our-mission-slide.jpg\" alt=\"The Mission Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"222px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/our-mission-slide.jpg 2x\"></a>\n<figcaption>Use the critical mission slide like this one in <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/business-plan/21284922?s_rank=7\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\">Business Plan</a> to capture that single, central idea that drives everything that you do.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n<h3>2. The SWOT Slide</h3>\n<p>Strengths, weaknesses, opportunities, and threats: <em>they exist for every business. Considering them properly is crucial.</em> That's why they're condensed into a key idea and common approach called a SWOT.</p>\n<p>You'll find a SWOT analysis slide in many PPT for marketing templates. Use a SWOT and fill it out to show proper consideration of each force in your business.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/marketing-plan-powerpoint-presentation-TRCH4C\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/swot-analysis.jpg\" alt=\"SWOT Analysis in Marketing Plan\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"541px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/swot-analysis.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/swot-analysis.jpg\" alt=\"SWOT Analysis in Marketing Plan\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"406px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/swot-analysis.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/swot-analysis.jpg\" alt=\"SWOT Analysis in Marketing Plan\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"241px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/swot-analysis.jpg 2x\"></a>\n<figcaption>A SWOT analysis slide like this one in <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/marketing-plan-powerpoint-presentation-TRCH4C\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\">Marketing Plan</a> will help you show that you've considered each of the key forces for your business.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n<h3>3. The Team Slide</h3>\n<p>No matter what type of presentation you're building, showing off the team behind the work is a good idea. A team slide can make your co-workers feel celebrated and recognized, and it also builds familiarity with your audience. </p>\n<p>Almost all the marketing PowerPoint templates we've featured in this round-up will include a team slide. Use one of them in your marketing PowerPoint plan to \"put a name with a face\" for your audience.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/business-plan-powerpoint-presentation-template/18705880?s_rank=18\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/team-slide.jpg\" alt=\"The Team Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"498px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/team-slide.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/team-slide.jpg\" alt=\"The Team Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"374px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/team-slide.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/team-slide.jpg\" alt=\"The Team Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"222px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/team-slide.jpg 2x\"></a>\n<figcaption>The team slide in <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/business-plan-powerpoint-presentation-template/18705880?s_rank=18\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\">Business Plan</a> is the perfect example of showing off the members behind your hard work.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n<h3>4. The Map Slide</h3>\n<p>Most marketing plans need to include a geographic consideration. That might mean showing trends or specific plans that'll help you reach targeted audiences.</p>\n<p>That's why you want to use a map slide to do just that. Bringing specific geographics to life will help cement that there are specific, targeted plans. In the best marketing PowerPoint templates like the example below, you can see how to use a map slide.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/social-media-trends-powerpoint-template-YCBFE8\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/asia-map-analysis.jpg\" alt=\"Map Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"495px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/asia-map-analysis.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/asia-map-analysis.jpg\" alt=\"Map Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"372px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/asia-map-analysis.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/asia-map-analysis.jpg\" alt=\"Map Slide\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"221px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/151/posts/32766/image/asia-map-analysis.jpg 2x\"></a>\n<figcaption>Use a map slide like this one in <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/social-media-trends-powerpoint-template-YCBFE8\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener\">Social Media Trends</a> to help your audience connect the plans to specific areas.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n<h3>5. The Infographic Slide</h3>\n<p>Infographics can help you explain a process. Instead of just listing the steps in a process, use an infographic to make it highly visual.</p>\n<p>Your business plan should include some tactical plans. These are the specific steps it takes to execute the marketing plan. Those are best shown with infographics that illustrate ideas easily.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a Tips</h2>\n<p>Designing a great PPT marketing presentation takes not only strong ideas but refining them and putting those ideas into the best visual slides that tell a compelling story. </p>\n<p>You want to make your points stick with your audience and deliver them so that your key ideas that fit your marketing presentation goals.</p>\n<p><em>Here a few quick tips to help you do that:    </em></p>\n<h3>1. Focus Your PPT Marketing Message</h3>\n<p>Take your marketing topic and simplify it. Hone it down to connect with your audience boldly.</p>\n<p>Your goal is to get into the head of your audience. Think about how your topic will resonate with them. What question, statistic, or quick point could grab their attention right away?</p>\n<p>A good example of quick audience engagement is the question:</p>\n<p>“<em>What's the purpose of this email?</em>,” from the SlideShare presentation “<a href=\"https://www.slideshare.net/sendgrid/email-marketing-101-strategy\">Email Marketing 101: Strategy</a>,” by <a href=\"https://www.slideshare.net/sendgrid\" target=\"_self\">SendGrid</a>. This is then followed by another question: “<em>Or rather, what do you want your recipients to do?</em>”</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><iframe src=\"//www.slideshare.net/slideshow/embed_code/key/CTg9NjdXt0mxpX?startSlide=3\" width=\"850\" height=\"530\" frameborder=\"0\" scrolling=\"no\" loading=\"lazy\"> </iframe></figure>\n<p>These questions help draw the audience into your presentation topic, before they show potential purposes of email campaigns. Questions are a great way to lead your audience to a clear point.</p>\n<p>After you’ve got them hooked into your topic, then look to hold that attention throughout your marketing presentation before you end strong. Use Evidence to Prove Your Points</h3>\n<p>Whether from case studies, quality marketing studies, or your own research, real marketing data speaks to an audience better than generalizations or assumptions.</p>\n<p>While your logic and ideas can carry quite a bit of your presentation, showcasing a few key numbers inside easy-to-understand infographics will make your points more credible.</p>\n<p>Use a marketing PowerPoint template that comes with great infographic slides, like <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/the-digital-marketing-pro-powerpoint-template/19532544\">The Digital Marketing Pro</a> or the <a href=\"https://graphicriver.net/item/marketing-toolbox-powerpoint-template/19879042\">Marketing Toolbox</a>. Provide Clear, Actionable Takeaways</h3>\n<p>Great presentations tell a story that puts the spotlight on solving problems. They clarify with examples, but that information needs to make clear points that the audience can make use of.</p>\n<p>Provide takeaways throughout each section of your presentations—especially in your conclusion. You want your audience to be driven take notes, and recall your takeaways, so they can put your ideas into action.  </p>\n<p>There are some takeaways in the SlideShare “<a href=\"https://www.slideshare.net/slidecomet/5-storytelling-lessons-from-superhero-stories\" target=\"_self\">5 Storytelling Lessons From Superhero Stories</a>,” by <a href=\"https://www.slideshare.net/slidecomet\" target=\"_self\">HighSpark</a>. Format for Live vs Distributed Release</h3>\n<p>Before you jump into designing slides, be sure to consider: <em>how will you use the presentation deck you’re making?</em> Your presentation format will differ when giving a live presentation versus one that'll be distributed.</p>\n<p>In the live presentation case, you’ll want your slides to be concise, and support what you’ll be speaking. Your visuals need only compliment and highlight your key talking points. You can use impactful visuals, but it’s often best to keep text short and your points bold.</p>\n<p>Your presentation needs take a different approach when you’re making it for digital or online distribution. For example, if you’re designing a marketing presentation to be emailed to your team, or if you’ll be uploading your deck to SlideShare. In those cases, each slide in your presentation needs to communicate your point fully on its own, much like a PDF document would.</p>\n<p>Here are some great PowerPoint SlideShare examples you may help you get the most from your marketing PPT template:</p>\n<h3>1. Bright Colors</h3>\n<p>Using bright colors in the design of the marketing presentation template is on-trend. Many bright colors will make your presentation less boring and more fun. Using black or white text on bright colors also makes your text stand out.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/marketing-plan-template-B6DEU8D\" target=\"_self\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Bright%20Colors.jpg\" alt=\"Bright Colors\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"610px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Bright%20Colors.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Bright%20Colors.jpg\" alt=\"Bright Colors\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"457px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Bright%20Colors.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Bright%20Colors.jpg\" alt=\"Bright Colors\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"270px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Bright%20Colors.jpg 2x\"></a>\n<figcaption>This <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/marketing-plan-template-B6DEU8D\" target=\"_self\">marketing campaign template</a> from Envato Elements captures the audience's attention with the bright colors.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n<h3>2. Abstract Design</h3>\n<p>Having an abstract design in your marketing PowerPoint template is on-trend. It can make your presentation unique. An abstract design can engage for the audience without being distracting.</p>\n<h3>3. Infographics</h3>\n<p>Infographics are a great way to present data or text in an exciting way. Use an infographic to break up text. A  marketing PowerPoint presentation with less text becomes more engaging for the audience.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-marketing-powerpoint-template-7KXNFJ5\" target=\"_self\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Infographics.jpg\" alt=\"Infographics\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"570px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Infographics.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Infographics.jpg\" alt=\"Infographics\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"428px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Infographics.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Infographics.jpg\" alt=\"Infographics\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"253px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Infographics.jpg 2x\"></a>\n<figcaption>Colora is a business <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/business-marketing-powerpoint-template-7KXNFJ5\" target=\"_self\">marketing presentation PPT template</a> from Envato Elements that comes with infographics.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n<h3> 4. Color Gradient</h3>\n<p>A color gradient is where a color slowly transitions into another color. Use this design trend for any purpose. It can be bold or subtle.</p>\n<p>The color gradient could also be a part of the slide or just in the background. Having a gradient color is more interesting than just a single color on a slide. </p>\n<h3>5. Image Masking</h3>\n<p>When you can only see part of a full image that's called image masking. Many marketing PowerPoint templates already have this built in to the template. Most templates make it easy all you need to do is drag and drop the image into the placeholder.</p>\n<figure class=\"post_image\"><a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/digital-marketing-powerpoint-template-WQLCZJH\" target=\"_self\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=850/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Image%20masking.jpg\" alt=\"Image Masking\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"870px\" height=\"583px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-desktop\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1700/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Image%20masking.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=630/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Image%20masking.jpg\" alt=\"Image Masking\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"650px\" height=\"437px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-tablet\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=1260/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Image%20masking.jpg 2x\"><img src=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=360/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Image%20masking.jpg\" alt=\"Image Masking\" loading=\"lazy\" width=\"380px\" height=\"258px\" class=\"resized-image resized-image-mobile\" srcset=\"https://cms-assets.tutsplus.com/cdn-cgi/image/width=720/uploads/users/2533/posts/35749/image/Image%20masking.jpg 2x\"></a>\n<figcaption>This <a href=\"https://elements.envato.com/digital-marketing-powerpoint-template-WQLCZJH\" target=\"_self\">marketing presentation template </a>has several slides that feature image masking.</figcaption>\n</figure>\n<h2>Discover More PowerPoint Template Designs</h2>\n<p>So far, you’ve seen different marketing PowerPoint template designs that you can use as an inspiration or as a starting point for your presentation.
